2026-07-23T19:01:59.2572978Z ##[group]Run # Replace (not delete) non-alphanumeric characters so stripped punctuation never welds
2026-07-23T19:01:59.2573707Z [36;1m# Replace (not delete) non-alphanumeric characters so stripped punctuation never welds[0m
2026-07-23T19:01:59.2574340Z [36;1m# two words together (e.g. "rsksmart/rit-update" must not become "rsksmartrit-update"),[0m
2026-07-23T19:01:59.2574962Z [36;1m# then squeeze runs of spaces and trim, and cap length to keep the Slack message concise.[0m
2026-07-23T19:01:59.2575399Z [36;1msanitize() {[0m
2026-07-23T19:01:59.2575757Z [36;1m  printf '%s' "$1" | tr -c '[:alnum:]_ -' ' ' | tr -s ' ' | sed 's/^ *//;s/ *$//' | cut -c1-75[0m
2026-07-23T19:01:59.2576333Z [36;1m}[0m
2026-07-23T19:01:59.2576530Z [36;1m[0m
2026-07-23T19:01:59.2576872Z [36;1m# Write NAME=VALUE to GITHUB_ENV as a heredoc with a random delimiter, so a crafted[0m
2026-07-23T19:01:59.2577475Z [36;1m# value (e.g. a PR title containing newlines) can never inject additional variables.[0m
2026-07-23T19:01:59.2577901Z [36;1mwrite_env() {[0m
2026-07-23T19:01:59.2578217Z [36;1m  _delim="__EOF_$(od -An -N16 -tx1 /dev/urandom | tr -d ' \n')__"[0m
2026-07-23T19:01:59.2578562Z [36;1m  {[0m
2026-07-23T19:01:59.2578758Z [36;1m    echo "$1<<$_delim"[0m
2026-07-23T19:01:59.2579001Z [36;1m    echo "$2"[0m
2026-07-23T19:01:59.2579599Z [36;1m    echo "$_delim"[0m
2026-07-23T19:01:59.2579952Z [36;1m  } >> "$GITHUB_ENV"[0m
2026-07-23T19:01:59.2580175Z [36;1m}[0m
2026-07-23T19:01:59.2580353Z [36;1m[0m
2026-07-23T19:01:59.2580592Z [36;1mif [ "$GITHUB_EVENT_NAME" = pull_request ]; then[0m

2026-07-23T19:01:59.2582079Z [36;1m  # A PR title made up entirely of characters sanitize() replaces with spaces (e.g. only emoji)[0m
